They cite the ADR/PRD/bet that produced them and the code that implements them.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eRecords change only when the project itself changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eVolatile commitment layer (\u003ccode\u003ewiki/\u0026lt;scope\u0026gt;/{adrs,prds,epics,bets,constraints}/\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-volatile-commitment-layer-wikiscopeadrsprdsepicsbetsconstraints\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Volatile commitment layer (wiki/\u0026lt;scope\u0026gt;/{adrs,prds,epics,bets,constraints}/)\" href=\"#volatile-commitment-layer-wikiscopeadrsprdsepicsbetsconstraints\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese are human-approved or in-progress commitment-class artifacts. They are true \u003cem\u003eat the time they are written\u003c/em\u003e, but they become historical once the work is delivered:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eADRs\u003c/strong\u003e record the decision being made, the alternatives rejected, and the accepted consequences.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePRDs\u003c/strong\u003e describe the initiative — problem, appetite, fat-marker solution, no-gos, rabbit holes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEpics\u003c/strong\u003e group related work under a single outcome.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBets\u003c/strong\u003e are the commitments we actually make from the options — usually one per shaping cycle, linked to a PRD/ADR pair.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConstraints\u003c/strong\u003e are durable rules the project agrees to honor — architecture, UI, UX, language, workflow, security, performance. They shape what is allowed in every PRD/ADR/bet until explicitly retired.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" captures\u003c/strong\u003e are raw notes waiting to be triaged.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDeepdives\u003c/strong\u003e are transient repo inspections for  draft PRD / ADR / epic / bet\n         ↓\n   accepted PRD / ADR / epic / bet  ← commitment layer\n         ↓\n   implementation in the project repo\n         ↓\n   record in approval.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAccepted commitment artifacts authorize changes to the project repo.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConstraint check:\u003c/strong\u003e before accepting a PRD/ADR/epic/bet, verify it honors active \u003ccode\u003econstraints/\u003c/code\u003e in the scope. Flag violations and resolve them before acceptance.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOnce delivered, the useful residue is captured as a \u003cstrong\u003erecord\u003c/strong\u003e. The original ADR/PRD may then be archived or compacted into the record's history.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebrain:groom\u003c/code\u003e decays stale confidence, archives superseded commitments, and flags delivered work that needs a record.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebrain:links\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ebrain:state\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003ebrain:sync\u003c/code\u003e keep the permanent layer honest and navigable.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eUsing pi-brain for your own project\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-using-pi-brain-for-your-own-project\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Using pi-brain for your own project\" href=\"#using-pi-brain-for-your-own-project\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThere are three ways to start:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFork/clone this repo\u003c/strong\u003e on GitHub and customize it for your project. Or use the helper:\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"bash tools/clone-pi-brain.sh ~/projects/my-project-brain \u0026quot;My Org\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003ebash tools/clone-pi-brain.sh \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003e~\u003c/span\u003e/projects/my-project-brain \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eMy Org\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConvert an existing repo\u003c/strong\u003e with \u003ccode\u003e/brain:convert [subdir] [--dry-run]\u003c/code\u003e — moves the project code into \u003ccode\u003efiles/\u003c/code\u003e and makes the repo itself a pi-brain clone.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOnboard an external repo\u003c/strong\u003e with \u003ccode\u003e/brain:ingest-repo \u0026lt;path-or-url\u0026gt; [scope]\u003c/code\u003e — keeps the brain repo-agnostic. data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"org: \u0026quot;My Project\u0026quot;\nactive_repos:\n  - my-project\n  - my-project-ui\nconnectors:\n  github:\n    repos: []\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003erepos\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e[]\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe extension uses the current dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSources are immutable.\u003c/strong\u003e Snapshots and exports land in \u003ccode\u003esources/\u003c/code\u003e and are never 2Z"></path></svg></button></div><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned DirectoryRichtextContent-module__SharedMarkdownContent__hHXUL" data-hpc="true" containertiming="hpc"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">pi-brain 🧠🏠</h1><a id="user-content-pi-brain-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: pi-brain 🧠🏠" href="#pi-brain-"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/misabegovic/pi-brain/actions/workflows/validate.yml"><img src="https://github.com/misabegovic/pi-brain/actions/workflows/validate.yml/badge.svg" alt="Validate pi-brain" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@misabegovic/pi-brain" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c76732c98b820f3d674c87f35a93d308a8279c81308e31516f7a0daa157180f1/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f406d6973616265676f7669632f70692d627261696e" alt="npm" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/@misabegovic/pi-brain" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>A knowledge home for <a href="https://pi.dev" rel="nofollow">pi</a>.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">pi-brain is a self-contained, cloneable template for project- or customer-specific knowledge bases inside <a href="https://pi.dev" rel="nofollow">pi</a>. It is an <strong>intent store</strong>: it keeps the permanent layer of decisions, architecture, and product reasoning alongside the volatile layer of drafts, experiments, and AI suggestions. When volatile work is approved, it is promoted into the permanent layer and can then modify the actual project.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What it gives pi</h2><a id="user-content-what-it-gives-pi" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What it gives pi" href="#what-it-gives-pi"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Persistent working memory</strong> — every session starts with a glance at the project's briefing and tend queue.</li>
<li><strong>Natural-language capture</strong> — "note that we decided X" becomes an inbox item or wiki page.</li>
<li><strong>Question answering over the corpus</strong> — ask the project's brain, not just the current repo.</li>
<li><strong>Tend queue integration</strong> — see what queued up while you were away and digest it without leaving pi.</li>
<li><strong>Human-gated shaping</strong> — <code>/brain:shape</code> turns pitches into ADRs/PRDs with phase-end approval gates.</li>
<li><strong>A cozy theme</strong> — warm, low-contrast colors so long brain-tending sessions feel like home.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Vision: how pi-brain manages knowledge</h2><a id="user-content-vision-how-pi-brain-manages-knowledge" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Vision: how pi-brain manages knowledge" href="#vision-how-pi-brain-manages-knowledge"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">pi-brain separates knowledge into three layers:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Permanent layer (<code>wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/records/</code>)</h3><a id="user-content-permanent-layer-wikiscoperecords" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Permanent layer (wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/records/)" href="#permanent-layer-wikiscoperecords"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These describe the project <strong>as it actually is right now</strong>. They are the residue of delivered decisions and the source of truth for future work:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Records</strong> state the current, approved shape of a system, feature, or decision. They cite the ADR/PRD/bet that produced them and the code that implements them.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Records change only when the project itself changes.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Volatile commitment layer (<code>wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{adrs,prds,epics,bets,constraints}/</code>)</h3><a id="user-content-volatile-commitment-layer-wikiscopeadrsprdsepicsbetsconstraints" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Volatile commitment layer (wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{adrs,prds,epics,bets,constraints}/)" href="#volatile-commitment-layer-wikiscopeadrsprdsepicsbetsconstraints"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are human-approved or in-progress commitment-class artifacts. They are true <em>at the time they are written</em>, but they become historical once the work is delivered:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>ADRs</strong> record the decision being made, the alternatives rejected, and the accepted consequences.</li>
<li><strong>PRDs</strong> describe the initiative — problem, appetite, fat-marker solution, no-gos, rabbit holes.</li>
<li><strong>Epics</strong> group related work under a single outcome.</li>
<li><strong>Bets</strong> are the commitments we actually make from the options — usually one per shaping cycle, linked to a PRD/ADR pair.</li>
<li><strong>Constraints</strong> are durable rules the project agrees to honor — architecture, UI, UX, language, workflow, security, performance. They shape what is allowed in every PRD/ADR/bet until explicitly retired.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Raw / speculative layer (<code>wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{pitches,rfcs,ai-suggestions}/</code>, inbox, deepdives)</h3><a id="user-content-raw--speculative-layer-wikiscopepitchesrfcsai-suggestions-inbox-deepdives" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Raw / speculative layer (wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{pitches,rfcs,ai-suggestions}/, inbox, deepdives)" href="#raw--speculative-layer-wikiscopepitchesrfcsai-suggestions-inbox-deepdives"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fast, speculative, or AI-generated material that is allowed to be wrong:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Pitches</strong> are pre-bet ideas not yet shaped.</li>
<li><strong>RFCs</strong> are multi-perspective review documents — the conversation format between personas.</li>
<li><strong>AI-suggestions</strong> are agent-authored drafts awaiting human review.</li>
<li><strong>Inbox captures</strong> are raw notes waiting to be triaged.</li>
<li><strong>Deepdives</strong> are transient repo inspections for context.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Evidence layer (<code>wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{experiments,feedback}/</code>)</h3><a id="user-content-evidence-layer-wikiscopeexperimentsfeedback" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Evidence layer (wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/{experiments,feedback}/)" href="#evidence-layer-wikiscopeexperimentsfeedback"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Observations from the real world that inform decisions:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Experiments</strong> — A/B tests and other experiments with hypothesis, results, and decision.</li>
<li><strong>Feedback</strong> — user feedback, interviews, support signals, analytics observations.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Evidence pages feed into options, bets, and records.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Promotion path</h3><a id="user-content-promotion-path" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Promotion path" href="#promotion-path"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="inbox / deepdive / pitch
         ↓
   ai-suggestion (agent draft)
         ↓
   draft PRD / ADR / epic / bet
         ↓
   accepted PRD / ADR / epic / bet  ← commitment layer
         ↓
   implementation in the project repo
         ↓
   record in wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/records/  ← permanent layer"><pre class="notranslate"><code>inbox / deepdive / pitch
         ↓
   ai-suggestion (agent draft)
         ↓
   draft PRD / ADR / epic / bet
         ↓
   accepted PRD / ADR / epic / bet  ← commitment layer
         ↓
   implementation in the project repo
         ↓
   record in wiki/&lt;scope&gt;/records/  ← permanent layer
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Raw drafts never become truth without human approval.</li>
<li>Accepted commitment artifacts authorize changes to the project repo.</li>
<li><strong>Constraint check:</strong> before accepting a PRD/ADR/epic/bet, verify it honors active <code>constraints/</code> in the scope. Flag violations and resolve them before acceptance.</li>
<li>Once delivered, the useful residue is captured as a <strong>record</strong>. The original ADR/PRD may then be archived or compacted into the record's history.</li>
<li><code>brain:groom</code> decays stale confidence, archives superseded commitments, and flags delivered work that needs a record.</li>
<li><code>brain:links</code>, <code>brain:state</code>, and <code>brain:sync</code> keep the permanent layer honest and navigable.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Using pi-brain for your own project</h2><a id="user-content-using-pi-brain-for-your-own-project" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Using pi-brain for your own project" href="#using-pi-brain-for-your-own-project"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">There are three ways to start:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Fork/clone this repo</strong> on GitHub and customize it for your project. Or use the helper:
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bash tools/clone-pi-brain.sh ~/projects/my-project-brain &quot;My Org&quot;"><pre>bash tools/clone-pi-brain.sh <span class="pl-k">~</span>/projects/my-project-brain <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>My Org<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
</li>
<li><strong>Convert an existing repo</strong> with <code>/brain:convert [subdir] [--dry-run]</code> — moves the project code into <code>files/</code> and makes the repo itself a pi-brain clone.</li>
<li><strong>Onboard an external repo</strong> with <code>/brain:ingest-repo &lt;path-or-url&gt; [scope]</code> — keeps the brain repo-agnostic. The code stays outside the brain; only a lightweight metadata snapshot and wiki scaffold are created.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick start" href="#quick-start"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For a step-by-step checklist for real projects, see <a href="/misabegovic/pi-brain/blob/main/GETTING_STARTED.md">GETTING_STARTED.md</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Clone pi-brain as the starting point for a project/customer brain
git clone &lt;pi-brain&gt; my-project-brain &amp;&amp; cd my-project-brain

# Install the pi package (from npm or locally)
pi install @misabegovic/pi-brain
# or, when working on the template itself:
# pi install ./

# Bootstrap the local environment (Node check, pre-commit hook, health check)
bash tools/setup-local.sh

# Open pi inside the brain and run the setup wizard
pi
/brain:setup
/brain"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Clone pi-brain as the starting point for a project/customer brain</span>
git clone <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>pi-brain<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> my-project-brain <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-c1">cd</span> my-project-brain

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install the pi package (from npm or locally)</span>
pi install @misabegovic/pi-brain
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> or, when working on the template itself:</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> pi install ./</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Bootstrap the local environment (Node check, pre-commit hook, health check)</span>
bash tools/setup-local.sh

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Open pi inside the brain and run the setup wizard</span>
pi
/brain:setup
/brain</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Edit <code>brain.config.yml</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="org: &quot;My Project&quot;
active_repos:
  - my-project
  - my-project-ui
connectors:
  github:
    repos: []"><pre><span class="pl-ent">org</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>My Project<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-ent">active_repos</span>:
  - <span class="pl-s">my-project</span>
  - <span class="pl-s">my-project-ui</span>
<span class="pl-ent">connectors</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">github</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">repos</span>: <span class="pl-s">[]</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The extension uses the current project directory as the brain home by default. You can override with:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><code>PI_BRAIN_HOME</code> environment variable</li>
<li><code>.pi/brain-home</code> file in the current project (absolute path)</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Repository layout</h2><a id="user-content-repository-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Repository layout" href="#repository-layout"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="my-project-brain/
├── brain.config.yml      # org name + active repos + connectors
├── AGENTS.md             # rulebook the agent follows

│       ├── prds/         # volatile commitment: product requirement docs

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Commands</h2><a id="user-content-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Commands" href="#commands"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tools</h2><a id="user-content-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tools" href="#tools"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The extension registers these tools for the agent:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>brain_status</code> — read the status dashboard.</li>
<li><code>brain_capture</code> — append an item to the inbox.</li>
<li><code>brain_ask</code> — search the corpus with TF-IDF ranking over tokenized terms.</li>
<li><code>brain_tend</code> — list the inbox queue.</li>
<li><code>brain_validate</code> — validate wiki frontmatter.</li>
<li><code>brain_views</code> — regenerate the index view.</li>
<li><code>brain_sync</code> — validate + regenerate views.</li>
<li><code>brain_links</code> — derive the link graph.</li>
<li><code>brain_state</code> — regenerate state/roadmap/options pages.</li>
<li><code>brain_deepdive</code> — transiently inspect a target repo file/directory.</li>
<li><code>brain_ingest_repo</code> — onboard a repository as a maintained project.</li>
<li><code>brain_projects</code> — list onboarded projects.</li>
<li><code>brain_convert</code> — convert current repo into a pi-brain clone.</li>
<li><code>brain_pull_connectors</code> — run configured pull connectors.</li>
<li><code>brain_autonomy</code> — read or toggle autonomous brain-maintenance mode.</li>
<li><code>brain_ingest</code> — ingest a file, directory, or URL into <code>sources/</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Design principles</h2><a id="user-content-design-principles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Design principles" href="#design-principles"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Sources are immutable.</strong> Snapshots and exports land in <code>sources/</code> and are never rewritten.</li>
<li><strong>Wiki is the synthesis.</strong> The agent maintains <code>wiki/</code> with cited claims.</li>
<li><strong>No scheduled LLM runs.</strong> Work queues in <code>wiki/_state/inbox.md</code>; pi digests it when <em>you</em> choose to <code>/brain:tend</code>.</li>
<li><strong>Human-gated commitments.</strong> <code>/brain:shape</code> pauses for approval at phase boundaries.</li>
<li><strong>Confidence floor.</strong> Agent-authored content starts at <code>confidence: low</code> and cannot self-promote to <code>high</code> in the same change.</li>
<li><strong>Local-first.</strong> Each project/customer gets its own clone; no hosted tier required.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Git hook</h2><a id="user-content-git-hook" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Git hook" href="#git-hook"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Install the pre-commit hook manually:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cp tools/git-hooks/pre-commit .git/hooks/pre-commit"><pre>cp tools/git-hooks/pre-commit .git/hooks/pre-commit</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Or let <code>/brain:setup</code> install it for you. It runs <code>tools/brain-sync.mjs</code> before each commit to validate frontmatter and keep <code>wiki/index.md</code> fresh.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Testing</h2><a id="user-content-testing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Testing" href="#testing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="NODE_PATH=/path/to/pi-coding-agent/node_modules \
  node --import /path/to/jiti-register.mjs tests/load.test.ts"><pre>NODE_PATH=/path/to/pi-coding-agent/node_modules \
  node --import /path/to/jiti-register.mjs tests/load.test.ts</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Roadmap</h2><a id="user-content-roadmap" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Roadmap" href="#roadmap"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">pi-brain-specific evolutions — multi-repo aggregation, connector producers, richer TUI widgets, and customer packaging — are tracked in this repo's own <code>wiki/</code> as the shell is inhabited.</p>
</article></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="prc-PageLayout-PaneWrapper-pHPop pr-2" style="--offset-header:0px;--spacing-row:var(--spacing-none);--spacing-column:var(--spacing-none)" data-is-hidden="false" data-position="end"><div class="prc-PageLayout-HorizontalDivider-JLVqp prc-PageLayout-PaneHorizontalDivider-9tbnE" data-component="PageLayout.HorizontalDivider" data-variant-narrow="none" data-variant-regular="none" data-position="end" style="--spacing-divider:var(--spacing-none);--spacing:var(--spacing-none)"></div><div class="prc-PageLayout-Pane-AyzHK" data-component="SplitPageLayout.Pane" style="--spacing:var(--spacing-normal);--pane-min-width:256px;--pane-max-width:calc(100vw - var(--pane-max-width-diff));--pane-width-size:var(--pane-width-large);--pane-width:320px"><rails-partial data-partial-name="codeViewRepoRoute.Sidebar" class="RailsPartial-module__d-contents__G5m4w">
